default='')\nparser.add_argument('--length',     type=int,   default=2000)\nparser.add_argument('--gpu',        type=int,   default=-1)\n\nargs = parser.parse_args()\n\nnp.random.seed(args.seed)\n\n# Variable, FunctionSet\nimport chainer.functions as F\nimport chainer.links as L\n\nclass CharRNN(FunctionSet):\n\n    def __init__(self, n_vocab, n_units):\n        super(CharRNN, self).__init__(\n            embed = F.EmbedID(n_vocab, n_units),\n            l1_x = L.Linear(n_units, 4*n_units),\n            l1_h = L.Linear(n_units, 4*n_units),\n            l2_h = L.Linear(n_units, 4*n_units),\n            l2_x = L.Linear(n_units, 4*n_units),\n            l3   = L.Linear(n_units, n_vocab),\n        )\n        for param in self.parameters:\n            param[:] = np.random.uniform(-0.08, 0.08, param.shape)\n\n    def forward_one_step(self, x_data, y_data, state, train=True, dropout_ratio=0.5):\n        x = Variable(x_data, volatile=not train)\n        t = Variable(y_data, volatile=not train)\n\n        h0      = self.embed(x)\n        h1_in   = self.l1_x(F.dropout(h0, ratio=dropout_ratio, train=train)) + self.l1_h(state['h1'])\n        c1, h1  = F.lstm(state['c1'], h1_in)\n        h2_in   = self.l2_x(F.dropout(h1, ratio=dropout_ratio, train=train)) + self.l2_h(state['h2'])\n        c2, h2  = F.lstm(state['c2'], h2_in)\n        y       = self.l3(F.dropout(h2, ratio=dropout_ratio, train=train))\n        state   = {'c1': c1, 'h1': h1, 'c2': c2, 'h2': h2}\n\n        if train:\n            return state, F.softmax_cross_entropy(y, t)\n        else:\n            return state, F.softmax(y)\n\ndef make_initial_state(n_units, batchsize=50, train=True):\n    return {name: Variable(np.zeros((batchsize, n_units), dtype=np.float32),\n            volatile=not train)\n            for name in ('c1', 'h1', 'c2', 'h2')}\n\n\n\n\ntrain_mecab.py \u3067 \u30d5\u30a1\u30a4\u30eb\u540d\u6307\u5b9a\u306a\u3057\u306e\u30c7\u30d5\u30a9\u30eb\u30c8 \u5b9f\u884c\u30a8\u30e9\u30fc\u306a\u304f\uff08\u7e70\u308a\u8fd4\u3057\u6210\u529f\uff09\u884c\u3046\u3053\u3068\u304c\u3067\u304d\u307e\u3057\u305f\u3002\n\n\n\u6700\u7d42\u7684\u306b\u52d5\u4f5c\u6210\u529f\u3057\u305f\u30d5\u30a1\u30a4\u30eb\u8cc7\u6e90\n\n\ntrain_mecab.py\n# coding:utf-8\n\nimport time\nimport math\nimport sys\nimport argparse\nimport cPickle as pickle\nimport copy\nimport os\nimport codecs\nimport MeCab\n\nimport numpy as np\nfrom chainer import cuda, Variable, FunctionSet, optimizers\nimport chainer.functions as F\nfrom CharRNN import CharRNN, make_initial_state\n\n# input data\ndef load_data(args):\n    vocab = {}\n    print ('%s/input.txt'% args.data_dir)\n    f_words = open(\"{dir_name}/{file_name}\".format(dir_name=args.data_dir, file_name=args.file_name), 'r')\n    mt = MeCab.Tagger('-Ochasen')\n\n    words = []\n    for line in f_words:\n        result = mt.parseToNode(line)\n        while result:\n            words.append(unicode(result.surface, 'utf-8'))\n            result = result.next\n    dataset = np.ndarray((len(words),), dtype=np.int32)\n\n    for i, word in enumerate(words):\n        if word not in vocab:\n            vocab[word] = len(vocab)\n    print 'corpus length:', len(words)\n    print 'vocab size:', len(vocab)\n    return dataset, words, vocab\n\n# arguments\nparser = argparse.ArgumentParser()\nparser.add_argument('--data_dir',                   type=str,   default='data/corpus')\nparser.add_argument('--file_name',                  type=str,   default='asuka.txt')\nparser.add_argument('--checkpoint_dir',             type=str,   default='learned_models')\nparser.add_argument('--gpu',                        type=int,   default=-1)\nparser.add_argument('--rnn_size',                   type=int,   default=128)\nparser.add_argument('--learning_rate',              type=float, default=2e-3)\nparser.add_argument('--learning_rate_decay',        type=float, default=0.97)\nparser.add_argument('--learning_rate_decay_after',  type=int,   default=10)\nparser.add_argument('--decay_rate',                 type=float, default=0.95)\nparser.add_argument('--dropout',                    type=float, default=0.0)\nparser.add_argument('--seq_length',                 type=int,   default=50)\nparser.add_argument('--batchsize',                  type=int,   default=50)\nparser.add_argument('--epochs',                     type=int,   default=50)\nparser.add_argument('--grad_clip',                  type=int,   default=5)\nparser.add_argument('--init_from',                  type=str,   default='')\n\nargs = parser.parse_args()\n\nif not os.path.exists(args.checkpoint_dir):\n    os.mkdir(args.checkpoint_dir)\n\nn_epochs    = args.epochs\nn_units     = args.rnn_size\nbatchsize   = args.batchsize\nbprop_len   = args.seq_length\ngrad_clip   = args.grad_clip\n\ntrain_data, words, vocab = load_data(args)\n\n\"\"\"\n\u4ee5\u4e0b\u3092\u5909\u66f4\n\n(\u76ee\u7684\uff09sample.py\u5b9f\u884c\u6642\u3001ValueError: 'wb'))\n\n(\u4ee5\u4e0b\u306f\u5909\u66f4\u5f8c )\n(\u5909\u66f4\u70b91)  protocol=1 \u3092 \u8ffd\u52a0\n(\u5909\u66f4\u70b92)  dump\u30e1\u30bd\u30c3\u30c9\u3067\u306a\u304f\u3001dumps\u30e1\u30bd\u30c3\u30c9\u4f7f\u7528\u3059\u308b\u5834\u5408\u3001dumps\u306f\u30d5\u30a1\u30a4\u30eb\u51fa\u529b\u5148\u5f15\u6570\u3092\u53d7\u3051\u53d6\u3089\u306a\u3044\u305f\u3081\u3001\u4e00\u5ea6\u3001dump\u30d5\u30a1\u30a4\u30eb\u3092obj\u5909\u6570\u306b\u683c\u7d0d\u3057\u3001obj\u3092\u30d5\u30a1\u30a4\u30eb\u51fa\u529b\u3059\u308b\n\nvocab_dump_object = pickle.dumps(vocab, open('%s/vocab.bin'%args.data_dir, 'wb') protocol=1)\n\nvocab_file_name = '%s/vocab.bin'%args.data_dir \n\nwith codecs.open(vocab_file_name, \"wb\") as f:\n    f.write(vocab_dump_object)\n\nf.close()\n\n\"\"\"\n#pickle.dumps(vocab, open('%s/vocab.bin'%args.data_dir, 'wb'), protocol=1)\n\nvocab_dump_object = pickle.dumps(vocab, protocol=1)\n\nvocab_file_name = '%s/vocab.bin'%args.data_dir \n\nwith codecs.open(vocab_file_name, 'wb') as f:\n    f.write(vocab_dump_object)\n\nf.close()\n\nif len(args.init_from) > 0:\n    model = pickle.load(open(args.init_from, 'rb'))\nelse:\n    model = CharRNN(len(vocab), n_units)\n\nif args.gpu >= 0:\n    cuda.get_device(args.gpu).use()\n    model.to_gpu()\n\noptimizer = optimizers.RMSprop(lr=args.learning_rate, alpha=args.decay_rate, eps=1e-8)\noptimizer.setup(model)\n\nwhole_len    = train_data.shape[0]\njump         = whole_len / batchsize\nepoch        = 0\nstart_at     = time.time()\ncur_at       = start_at\nstate        = make_initial_state(n_units, batchsize=batchsize)\nif args.gpu >= 0:\n    accum_loss   = Variable(cuda.zeros(()))\n    for key, value in state.items():\n        value.data = cuda.to_gpu(value.data)\nelse:\n    accum_loss   = Variable(np.zeros((), dtype=np.float32))\n\nprint 'going to train {} iterations'.format(jump * n_epochs)\nfor i in xrange(jump * n_epochs):\n    x_batch = np.array([train_data[(jump * j + i) % whole_len]\n                        for j in xrange(batchsize)])\n    y_batch = np.array([train_data[(jump * j + i + 1) % whole_len]\n                        for j in xrange(batchsize)])\n\n    if args.gpu >=0:\n        x_batch = cuda.to_gpu(x_batch)\n        y_batch = cuda.to_gpu(y_batch)\n\n    state, loss_i = model.forward_one_step(x_batch, y_batch, state, dropout_ratio=args.dropout)\n    accum_loss   += loss_i\n\n    if (i + 1) % bprop_len == 0:  # Run truncated BPTT\n        now = time.time()\n        print '{}/{}, train_loss = {}, time = {:.2f}'.format((i+1)/bprop_len, jump, accum_loss.data / bprop_len, now-cur_at)\n        cur_at = now\n\n        optimizer.zero_grads()\n        accum_loss.backward()\n        accum_loss.unchain_backward()  # truncate\n        if args.gpu >= 0:\n            accum_loss = Variable(cuda.zeros(()))\n        else:\n            accum_loss = Variable(np.zeros((), dtype=np.float32))\n\n        optimizer.clip_grads(grad_clip)\n        optimizer.update()\n\n    if (i + 1) % 10 == 0:\n        fn = ('%s/charrnn_epoch_%.2f.chainermodel' % (args.checkpoint_dir, float(i)/jump))\n        pickle.dump(copy.deepcopy(model).to_cpu(), open(fn, 'wb'))\n        pickle.dump(copy.deepcopy(model).to_cpu(), open('%s/latest.chainermodel'%(args.checkpoint_dir), 'wb'))\n\n    if (i + 1) % jump == 0:\n        epoch += 1\n\n        if epoch >= args.learning_rate_decay_after:\n            optimizer.lr *= args.learning_rate_decay\n            print 'decayed learning rate by a factor {} to {}'.format(args.learning_rate_decay, optimizer.lr)\n\n    sys.stdout.flush()\n\n\n\nsample.py\n#%%\nimport = np.array([0], dtype=np.int32)\nif args.gpu >= 0:\n    prev_char = cuda.to_gpu(prev_char)\n\nif len(args.primetext) > 0:\n    for i in unicode(args.primetext, 'utf-8'):\n        sys.stdout.write(i)\n prev_char, state, train=False)\n\nfor i in xrange(args.length):\n    state, prob = model.forward_one_step(prev_char, prev_char, state, train=False)\n\n    if args.sample > 0:\n        probability = np.random.choice(range(len(probability)), p=probability)\n    else:\n        index = np.argmax(cuda.to_cpu(prob.data))\n    sys.stdout.write(ivocab[index])\n\n    prev_char = np.array([index], \u3092 \u6e21\u3059\n\n\n\nsample.py\uff08\u629c\u7c8b\uff09\n\nparser.add_argument('--vocabulary', type=str,   required=True)\n\n\n\uff08 \u4e2d\u7565 \uff09\n\n\n# load vocabulary\nvocab = pickle.load(open(args.vocabulary, 'rb'))\nivocab = {}\nfor c, i in vocab.items():\n   ivocab[i] = c\n\n\n\n\n\n\nsample.py\uff08\u629c\u7c8b\uff09\nfor i in xrange(args.length):\n   state, prob = model.forward_one_step(prev_char, prev_char, state, train=False)\n\n   if args.sample > 0:\n       probability = cuda.to_cpu(prob.data)[0].astype(np.float64)\n       probability /= np.sum(probability)\n       index = np.random.choice(range(len(probability)), p=probability)\n   else:\n       index = np.argmax(cuda.to_cpu(prob.data))\n   sys.stdout.write(ivocab[index])\n\n   prev_char = np.array([index], dtype=np.int32)\n   if args.gpu >= 0:\n       prev_char = cuda.to_gpu(prev_char)\n\n\n\n\n\n\u3010 \u53c2\u8003 \u3011RNN / LSTM \u6587\u7ae0\u751f\u6210\u30bf\u30b9\u30af\n\n\u4ee5\u4e0b\u306e\u30a6\u30a7\u30d6\u30da\u30fc\u30b8\u3067\u306f\u3001Chainer \u540c\u68b1 \u306e \u6587\u7ae0\u751f\u6210\u30bf\u30b9\u30af os\nimport codecs\nimport MeCab\n\nimport numpy as np\nfrom chainer import cuda, Variable, FunctionSet, optimizers\nimport chainer.functions as F\nfrom CharRNN import CharRNN, make_initial_state\n\n# input data\ndef load_data(args):\n    vocab = {}\n    print ('%s/input.txt'% args.data_dir)\n    f_words = open(\"{dir_name}/{file_name}\".format(dir_name=args.data_dir, file_name=args.file_name), 'r')\n    mt = MeCab.Tagger('-Ochasen')\n    \n    words = []\n    for line in f_words:\n        result = mt.parseToNode(line)\n        while result:\n            words.append(unicode(result.surface, 'utf-8'))\n            result = result.next\n    dataset = np.ndarray((len(words),), dtype=np.int32)\n\n    for i, word in enumerate(words):\n        if word not in vocab:\n            vocab[word] = len(vocab)\n    print 'corpus length:', len(words)\n    print 'vocab size:', len(vocab)\n    return dataset, words, vocab\n\n# arguments\nparser = argparse.ArgumentParser()\nparser.add_argument('--data_dir',                   type=str,   default='data/corpus')\nparser.add_argument('--file_name',                  type=str,   default='input.txt')\nparser.add_argument('--checkpoint_dir',             type=str,   default='learned_models')\nparser.add_argument('--gpu',                        type=int,   default=-1)\nparser.add_argument('--rnn_size',                   type=int,   default=128)\nparser.add_argument('--learning_rate',              type=float, default=2e-3)\nparser.add_argument('--learning_rate_decay',        type=float, default=0.97)\nparser.add_argument('--learning_rate_decay_after',  type=int,   default=10)\nparser.add_argument('--decay_rate',                 type=float, default=0.95)\nparser.add_argument('--dropout',                    type=float, default=0.0)\nparser.add_argument('--seq_length',                 type=int,   default=50)\nparser.add_argument('--batchsize',                  type=int,   default=50)\nparser.add_argument('--epochs',                     type=int,   default=50)\nparser.add_argument('--grad_clip',                  type=int,   default=5)\nparser.add_argument('--init_from',                  type=str,   default='')\n\nargs = parser.parse_args()\n\nif not os.path.exists(args.checkpoint_dir):\n    os.mkdir(args.checkpoint_dir)\n\nn_epochs    = args.epochs\nn_units     = args.rnn_size\nbatchsize   = args.batchsize\nbprop_len   = args.seq_length\ngrad_clip   = args.grad_clip\n\ntrain_data, words, vocab = load_data(args)\npickle.dump(vocab, open('%s/vocab.bin'%args.data_dir, 'wb'))\n\nif len(args.init_from) > 0:\n    model = pickle.load(open(args.init_from, 'rb'))\nelse:\n    model = CharRNN(len(vocab), n_units)\n\nif args.gpu >= 0:\n    cuda.get_device(args.gpu).use()\n    model.to_gpu()\n\noptimizer = optimizers.RMSprop(lr=args.learning_rate, alpha=args.decay_rate, eps=1e-8)\noptimizer.setup(model)\n\nwhole_len    = train_data.shape[0]\njump         = whole_len / batchsize\nepoch        = 0\nstart_at     = time.time()\ncur_at       = start_at\nstate        = make_initial_state(n_units, batchsize=batchsize)\nif args.gpu >= 0:\n    accum_loss   = Variable(cuda.zeros(()))\n    for key, value in state.items():\n        value.data = cuda.to_gpu(value.data)\nelse:\n    accum_loss   = Variable(np.zeros((), dtype=np.float32))\n\nprint 'going to train {} iterations'.format(jump * n_epochs)\nfor i in xrange(jump * n_epochs):\n    x_batch = np.array([train_data[(jump * j + i) % whole_len]\n                        for j in xrange(batchsize)])\n    y_batch = np.array([train_data[(jump * j + i + 1) % whole_len]\n                        for j in xrange(batchsize)])\n\n    if args.gpu >=0:\n        x_batch = cuda.to_gpu(x_batch)\n        y_batch = cuda.to_gpu(y_batch)\n\n    state, loss_i = model.forward_one_step(x_batch, y_batch, state, dropout_ratio=args.dropout)\n    accum_loss   += loss_i\n\n    if (i + 1) % bprop_len == 0:  # Run truncated BPTT\n        now = time.time()\n        print '{}/{}, train_loss = {}, time = {:.2f}'.format((i+1)/bprop_len, jump, accum_loss.data / bprop_len, now-cur_at)\n        cur_at = now\n\n        optimizer.zero_grads()\n        accum_loss.backward()\n        accum_loss.unchain_backward()  # truncate\n        if args.gpu >= 0:\n            accum_loss = Variable(cuda.zeros(()))\n        else:\n            accum_loss = Variable(np.zeros((), dtype=np.float32))\n\n        optimizer.clip_grads(grad_clip)\n        optimizer.update()\n\n    if (i + 1) % 10 == 0:\n        fn = ('%s/charrnn_epoch_%.2f.chainermodel' % (args.checkpoint_dir, float(i)/jump))\n        pickle.dump(copy.deepcopy(model).to_cpu(), open(fn, 'wb'))\n        pickle.dump(copy.deepcopy(model).to_cpu(), open('%s/latest.chainermodel'%(args.checkpoint_dir), 'wb'))\n\n    if (i + 1) % jump == 0:\n        epoch += 1\n\n        if epoch >= args.learning_rate_decay_after:\n            optimizer.lr *= args.learning_rate_decay\n            print 'decayed learning rate by a factor {} to {}'.format(args.learning_rate_decay, optimizer.lr)\n\n    sys.stdout.flush()\n```\n\n####__\u4e8b\u5f8c\u8ffd\u8a18__\n___\n\ntrain_mecab.py \u306e \u4ee5\u4e0b \u306f\u3001\n\n> print('%s/input.txt'% \u306f\u3001Git clone\u3057\u305f\u5143\u306e\u30d5\u30a1\u30a4\u30eb\u3092\u305d\u306e\u307e\u307e\u4f7f\u3044\u307e\u3059__\n\n* __sample.py__\n\n```{Python:Python}\nimport time\nimport math\nimport sys\nimport argparse\nimport cPickle as pickle\nimport codecs\n\nimport numpy as np\nfrom chainer import cuda, Variable, FunctionSet\nimport chainer.functions as F\nfrom CharRNN import CharRNN, make_initial_state\n\nsys.stdout = codecs.getwriter('utf_8')(sys.stdout)\n\n#%% arguments\nparser = argparse.ArgumentParser()\n\nparser.add_argument('--model',      type=str,   required=True)\nparser.add_argument('--vocabulary', type=str,   required=True)\nparser.add_argument('--seed',       type=int,   default=123)\nparser.add_argument('--sample',     type=int,   default=1)\nparser.add_argument('--primetext',  type=str,   default='')\nparser.add_argument('--length',     type=int,   default=2000)\nparser.add_argument('--gpu',        type=int,   default=-1)\n\nargs = parser.parse_args()\n\nnp.random.seed(args.seed)\n\n# load vocabulary\nvocab = pickle.load(open(args.vocabulary, 'rb'))\nivocab = {}\nfor c, i in vocab.items():\n    ivocab[i] = c\n\n# load model\nmodel = pickle.load(open(args.model, 'rb'))\nn_units = model.embed.W.data.shape[1]\n\nif args.gpu >= 0:\n    cuda.get_device(args.gpu).use()\n    model.to_gpu()\n\n# initialize generator\nstate = make_initial_state(n_units, batchsize=1, train=False)\nif args.gpu >= 0:\n    for key, value in state.items():\n        value.data = cuda.to_gpu(value.data)\n\nprev_char = np.array([0], dtype=np.int32)\nif args.gpu >= 0:\n    prev_char = cuda.to_gpu(prev_char)\n\nif len(args.primetext) > 0:\n    for i in unicode(args.primetext, 'utf-8'):\n        sys.stdout.write(i)\n        prev_char = np.ones((1,), dtype=np.int32) * vocab[i]\n        if args.gpu >= 0:\n            prev_char = cuda.to_gpu(prev_char)\n\n        state, prob = model.forward_one_step(prev_char, prev_char, state, train=False)\n\nfor i in xrange(args.length):\n    state, prob = model.forward_one_step(prev_char, prev_char, state, train=False)\n\n    if args.sample > 0:\n        probability = cuda.to_cpu(prob.data)[0].astype(np.float64)\n        probability /= np.sum(probability)\n        index = np.random.choice(range(len(probability)), p=probability)\n    else:\n        index = np.argmax(cuda.to_cpu(prob.data))\n    sys.stdout.write(ivocab[index])\n\n    prev_char = np.array([index], dtype=np.int32)\n    if args.gpu >= 0:\n        prev_char = cuda.to_gpu(prev_char)\n\n\nprint\n```\n\n* __CharRNN.py__\n\n```{Python:Python}\nimport numpy as np\nfrom chainer import Variable, FunctionSet\nimport chainer.functions as F\nimport chainer.links as L\n\nclass CharRNN(FunctionSet):\n\n    def __init__(self, n_vocab, n_units):\n        super(CharRNN, self).__init__(\n            embed = F.EmbedID(n_vocab, n_units),\n            l1_x = L.Linear(n_units, 4*n_units),\n            l1_h = L.Linear(n_units, 4*n_units),\n            l2_h = L.Linear(n_units, 4*n_units),\n            l2_x = L.Linear(n_units, 4*n_units),\n            l3   = L.Linear(n_units, n_vocab),\n        )\n        for param in self.parameters:\n            param[:] = np.random.uniform(-0.08, 0.08, param.shape)\n\n    def forward_one_step(self, x_data, y_data, state, train=True, dropout_ratio=0.5):\n        x = Variable(x_data, volatile=not train)\n        t = Variable(y_data, volatile=not train)\n\n        h0      = self.embed(x)\n        h1_in   = self.l1_x(F.dropout(h0, ratio=dropout_ratio, train=train)) + self.l1_h(state['h1'])\n        c1, h1  = F.lstm(state['c1'], h1_in)\n        h2_in   = self.l2_x(F.dropout(h1, ratio=dropout_ratio, train=train)) + self.l2_h(state['h2'])\n        c2, h2  = F.lstm(state['c2'], h2_in)\n        y       = self.l3(F.dropout(h2, ratio=dropout_ratio, train=train))\n        state   = {'c1': c1, 'h1': h1, 'c2': c2, 'h2': h2}\n\n        if train:\n            return state, F.softmax_cross_entropy(y, t)\n        else:\n            return state, F.softmax(y)\n\ndef make_initial_state(n_units, batchsize=50, train=True):\n    return {name: Variable(np.zeros((batchsize, n_units), dtype=np.float32),\n            volatile=not train)\n            for name in ('c1', 'h1', 'c2', 'h2')}\n```\n\n___\n\n####__train_mecab.py \u3067 \u30d5\u30a1\u30a4\u30eb\u540d\u6307\u5b9a\u306a\u3057\u306e\u30c7\u30d5\u30a9\u30eb\u30c8 \u5b66\u7fd2\u30b3\u30fc\u30d1\u30b9 np.ndarray((len(words),), dtype=np.int32)\n\n    for i, word in enumerate(words):\n        if word not in vocab:\n            vocab[word] = len(vocab)\n    print 'corpus length:', len(words)\n    print 'vocab size:', len(vocab)\n    return dataset, words, vocab\n\n# arguments\nparser = argparse.ArgumentParser()\nparser.add_argument('--data_dir',                   type=str, ('%s/charrnn_epoch_%.2f.chainermodel' % (args.checkpoint_dir, float(i)/jump))\n        pickle.dump(copy.deepcopy(model).to_cpu(), open(fn, 'wb'))\n        pickle.dump(copy.deepcopy(model).to_cpu(), open('%s/latest.chainermodel'%(args.checkpoint_dir), 'wb'))\n\n    if (i + 1) % jump == 0:\n        epoch += 1\n\n        if epoch >= args.learning_rate_decay_after:\n            optimizer.lr *= args.learning_rate_decay\n            print 'decayed learning rate by a factor {} to {}'.format(args.learning_rate_decay, optimizer.lr)\n\n    sys.stdout.flush()\n```\n\n###sample.py\n\n```{Python:sample.py}\n#%%\nimport time\nimport math\nimport sys\nimport argparse\nimport cPickle as pickle\nimport codecs\n\nimport numpy as np\nfrom chainer import cuda, Variable, FunctionSet\nimport chainer.functions as F\nfrom CharRNN import CharRNN, make_initial_state\n\nsys.stdout = codecs.getwriter('utf_8')(sys.stdout)\n\n#%% arguments\nparser = argparse.ArgumentParser()\n\nparser.add_argument('--model',      type=str,   required=True)\nparser.add_argument('--vocabulary', type=str,   required=True)\n\nparser.add_argument('--seed',       type=int,   default=123)\nparser.add_argument('--sample',     type=int,   default=1)\nparser.add_argument('--primetext',  type=str,   default='')\nparser.add_argument('--length',     type=int,   default=2000)\nparser.add_argument('--gpu',        type=int,   default=-1)\n\nargs = parser.parse_args()\n\nnp.random.seed(args.seed)\n\n# model.embed.W.data.shape[1]\n\nif args.gpu >= 0:\n    cuda.get_device(args.gpu).use()\n    model.to_gpu()\n\n# initialize generator\nstate = make_initial_state(n_units, batchsize=1, train=False)\nif args.gpu >= 0:\n    for key, value in state.items():\n        value.data = cuda.to_gpu(value.data)\n\nprev_char = np.array([0], dtype=np.int32)\nif args.gpu >= 0:\n    prev_char = cuda.to_gpu(prev_char)\n\nif len(args.primetext) > 0:\n    for i in unicode(args.primetext, 'utf-8'):\n        sys.stdout.write(i)\n        prev_char = np.ones((1,), dtype=np.int32) * vocab[i]\n state, prob = model.forward_one_step(prev_char, prev_char, state, train=False)\n\n    if args.sample > 0:\n        probability = cuda.to_cpu(prob.data)[0].astype(np.float64)\n        probability /= np.sum(probability)\n        index = np.random.choice(range(len(probability)), p=probability)\n    else:\n        index = np.argmax(cuda.to_cpu(prob.data))\n    sys.stdout.write(ivocab[index])\n\n    prev_char = np.array([index], dtype=np.int32)\n    if args.gpu >= 0:\n        prev_char = cuda.to_gpu(prev_char)\n\nprint\n```\n\n#__\u5b9f\u884c\u7d50\u679c__\n\n###__\u5b66\u7fd2\u30b3\u30fc\u30d1\u30b9\uff1a shakespeare vocabulary\n>vocab = pickle.load(open(args.vocabulary, 'rb'))\n>ivocab = {}\n>for c, i in vocab.items():\n>    ivocab[i] = c\n>```\n\n___\n\n>```{Python:sample.py\uff08\u629c\u7c8b\uff09}\n>for i in xrange(args.length):\n>    state, prob = model.forward_one_step(prev_char, prev_char, state, train=False)\n>\n>    if args.sample > 0:\n>        probability = cuda.to_cpu(prob.data)[0].astype(np.float64)\n>        probability /= np.sum(probability)\n>        index = np.random.choice(range(len(probability)), p=probability)\n>    else:\n>        index = np.argmax(cuda.to_cpu(prob.data))\n>    sys.stdout.write(ivocab[index])\n>\n>    prev_char = np.array([index], dtype=np.int32)\n>    if args.gpu >= 0:\n>        prev_char = cuda.to_gpu(prev_char)\n>```\n\n___\n\n##__\u3010 \u53c2\u8003 \u3011RNN / LSTM
